msg:At the end of the Spring Festival holiday, I brought my family to Jiaxing for a trip. I chose Haili. The experience when I checked in was good. The front desk staff were nice and the processing was fast. The room was 50 square meters. This price can be said to be very cost-effective. Haili's location is relatively remote in the whole Jiaxing. There are Qiyuan and Guanhaiyuan nearby. If you go there from Shanghai, you can take the children to Dongxing Dairy Farm to feed the cows. You should be able to milk there in the afternoon. We arrived in the morning and did not participate.
The buffet dinner is neither good nor bad. I will give you a price-performance ratio. The category is not particularly rich. You can try the small hot pot with children and the elderly. Although there are not many types, it is also okay to eat hot pot. The variety of desserts is relatively rich, and the brands of drinks are really average.
When we were leaving, the child may have accidentally knocked over a glass water cup and it broke without us noticing. The hotel called me and said that they would compensate me 20 yuan, which is not expensive, but it is indeed surprising for a five-star hotel. This hotel clearly told me that they would deduct the fee, and because it was the Spring Festival, there was no need to communicate back and forth. The staff said that it would be deducted from the Ctrip deposit, so I agreed and hung up the phone. Not long after, I received a second call from someone who should be a Ctrip staff member, telling me that the money had been negotiated and I didn‚Äôt have to pay, and the matter came to an end.
